text-align: justify;\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">IBC code requires that\ntoxic and carcinogenic vapors must not be vented to atmosphere while loading,\nbut must be returned to shore.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">IMO recommends that\nmaximum tank pressure should be 80% ( 1600mm )of the set pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If VRS has to be used ,\nthen the pressure drop calculations must be completed before arrival. The class\napproved vapour control system manuals should be on board, along with sample\ncalculations. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The ship should choose\nthe maximum loading rate for the cargo and then calculate the drop to ensure\nthat the system is capable of effectively delivering all vapour back to the\nshore tanks. There will be a meeting between mate and the terminal to properly\nset the HP alarm at the shore facility vapor connection.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before using VRS in US\nports it is a good practise to make the officer/ crew familiar , explain the\nVRS class approved manual ,safety precautions, USCG regulations wrt vapour\nrecovery systems&nbsp; and then issue a\ncertificate in accordance with 33 CFR 154.94\u2014signed by master.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: justify;\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Xqftm4tcGTw/XKDBOVyagQI/AAAAAAABgdA/EYpzo5GaYeQRtCUHHLds7ZWlUcqSmPFdgCLcBGAs/s1600/vaxpour-line.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"491\" data-original-width=\"700\" height=\"448\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Xqftm4tcGTw/XKDBOVyagQI/AAAAAAABgdA/EYpzo5GaYeQRtCUHHLds7ZWlUcqSmPFdgCLcBGAs/s640/vaxpour-line.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vapor\nreturn calculations:<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Find out the VD of the\nchemical. Say for EDC it is 3.42. from your VCS manual use the graph drawn for\npressure drop in mm Aq on Y axis and loading rate in cum/ hr on the X axis. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Use the relevant curve\ndepending on the number of tanks loaded simultaneously\u2014to read off the pressure\ndrop . Multiply this with VD to get A.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Total pressure should\nbe PV valve setting 2000 mm Aq X 0.8 ---call this figure B.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Anytime the manifold\nvapor pressure exceeds B-A---then reduce the loading rate.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">DOP has a VD of 13.5 .\nit has a very high pressure drop.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vapor\ngrowth rate:--<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">As the vapors are\nremoved from cargo tank while loading, the evaporation of chemical in tank\ncontinues.&nbsp; This means that the vapor\nrecovered is loaded liquid volume plus evaporated volume. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The VP of a chemical is\nclosely connected to the BP. Chemicals having high VP evaporate more quickly\nthat substances with low VP.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Any information on VP\nmust be tagged to a temperature. At BP, VP = AP.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Concentration of gas\nvapors which can be produced in an enclosed space is \u2013<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">PPM=VP (mm Hg ) X 1300<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Using gasoline as a\nbaseline cargo with an assumed vapour growth rate of 25% the foll formula can\nbe used to determine the VGR of other cargoes<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">VGR = 1.25 X saturated\nVP at 155 deg F in psi/ 12.5<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On the VCS high\npressure alarm is set at 90% of 2000 mm Aq or 1800 mm Aq.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Low pressure alarm is\nset at -350mm Aq.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The last 1 metre of\nvapor piping before the ship's vapor connection must be painted R/Y/R with the\nred bands 10 cms wide. This means the middle yellow band is 80 cms wide. It\nmust be stencilled VAPOR in black letters.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-NLSbk09ZuFQ/XKDBWnfeuvI/AAAAAAABgdE/99y0FKZ0YxMiHdnEmIE8tLErGnUT9QU5QCLcBGAs/s1600/downrrload.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"225\" data-original-width=\"224\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-NLSbk09ZuFQ/XKDBWnfeuvI/AAAAAAABgdE/99y0FKZ0YxMiHdnEmIE8tLErGnUT9QU5QCLcBGAs/s320/downrrload.jpg\" width=\"318\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Each vapor connection\nflange of ship must have&nbsp; a permanently\nattached 0.5 inch dia stud at least one inch long projecting outwards from the\nflange face. The stud fits into a hole in the hose flange. This prevents liquid\nhose from being connected to vapor system.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">VCS must be capable of\ndischg vapor at 1.25 times the max transfer rate.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vapors are processed,\nincinerated or dispersed far away from ship.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vapors are recovered by\nrefrigeration, aBsorbsion in lean oil or aDsorbsion.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If your ship has to use\nVCS ensure the metal spool pieces are connected in good time\u2014if you do it at\nthe eleventh hour cargo operations may get delayed as often a couple of spools\ndo not fit well. Instead of fixed spool pieces upto 3 metre long flexibles are\nallowed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Always ensure the vapor\nlines are drained at the lowest point aft. If liquid builds up in vapor linethe\nflow of vapor could be restricted causing sudden increase of tank pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">USCG wants a VCS drill\nevery 6 months .Training of personnel and testing of systems&nbsp; must be done prior arrival port. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">As a minimum, the\nfollowing items of equipment should be located/demonstrated/explained.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pipelines, drains,\nPipeline bonding strips, labeling, Vapour Connection/Manifolds incl manual\nvalve, protection stud, Vapour &nbsp;Connection\ncolouring /paint, &nbsp;Individual tank\nisolation valves, Pressure monitoring points/devices/gauges and recorders, &nbsp;Closed gauging system including high level\nalarms, Independent High-High/Tank\nOverfill alarms, &nbsp;audible/visual alarms,\nP.V. protection devices associated with system, Ship\u2019s Oil Transfer Procedures\nnotice,&nbsp;&nbsp;Maximum allowable\ncargo transfer rate and maximum allowable venting rates for individual cargo\ntanks.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Read the VCS class\napproved manual. It will be a taken amiss if the mate is not familiar with\npressure drop calculations involving pipe friction factors and pipeline ID\nfor&nbsp; resistance coefficients as explained\nin the ships VCS manual. The groups of pipelines being from tank to spool,\nspool to manifold and at the vapor manifold.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">NOTE: A good VRS manual\nwill NOT require you to do below&nbsp;\ncalculations-- as all info can be lifted off the graphs- pressure drop\nversus loading rate , on curve or the target vapor specific gravity.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">VRS PD units\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">PD/ mm Aq<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Friction coeff factor/\n0.02 ( 0.017 to 0.022approx for a standard 20000 DWT chem. Tanker )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">MAX LIQUID PRESSURE AT\nMANIFOLD/ 10 KG</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before the pipework\nlosses can be established, the friction factor must be calculated. The friction\nfactor will be dependant on the pipe size, inner roughness of the pipe, flow\nvelocity and fluid viscosity. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Darcy friction\nfactor is a dimensionless number used in internal flow calculations. It\nexpresses the linear relationship between mean flow velocity and pressure\ngradient. The pipe diameter times the drop in pressure in the fluid due to\nfriction as it passes through the pipe, is divided by the product of the pipe\nlength and the kinetic energy of the fluid per unit volume. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">French engineer <span style=\"background-color: white;\">Henry\nDarcy\u2019s equation </span>is used&nbsp; to measure the\nPD through the PV&nbsp; in some VRS manuals . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Be aware that Darcy\u2019s\nFF is 4 times larger than British engineer Fannings FF which is used in some\nother manuals.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Test vacuum of the PV\nby using a graco pump to create a vacuum of 0.035 bars in the pipeline , till\nthe LP alarm rings. Test everything 24 hrs before .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vapour recovered\nashore= loaded liquid volume + evaporated vapor growth volume.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Shore VR hose designed\nto burst at 2 bars. At 2 psi vacuum , hose should not collapse.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">For chemical tankers (\nvapour +_air ) mixture density of 3.6 kg/ cum and VGR 1.2<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;will cover all chemicals except those with a\nRVP &gt; AP ( IBC code 15.14 ) <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ch Officer to fill up\nVRS Pre arr and Pre-operational checklist. At berth in pre-load meeting <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;find out if ship\u2019s tank pressure pushes gases\nout OR if shore is using a &nbsp;vacuum\u2014in\nwhich case if cargo stops suddenly there will be sever vacuum in ship\u2019s tanks.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Shore Vapor return hose\nmust have support.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Include Vapor return\nsystem in USCG oil transfer procedures. margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"240\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQToDoeqSoI/AAAAAAAABy0/1wGfu0MbOjY/s320/hurricane+photo.jpeg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div><br />\nVADAKAYIL INC is a brand at sea, in the parcel chemical tanker world.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRap5DmXz8I/AAAAAAAACZA/h01mhnE1E-g/s1600/octopussy.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRap5DmXz8I/AAAAAAAACZA/h01mhnE1E-g/s320/octopussy.JPG\" width=\"240\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Your personal brand is what people say about you, behind your back . Immortal words of Oscar Wilde: \"Be yourself, everyone else is already taken.\"<br />\n<br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQWEKvXUxNI/AAAAAAAABzI/tUNMT6aiSFM/s1600/sudden.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQWEKvXUxNI/AAAAAAAABzI/tUNMT6aiSFM/s1600/sudden.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">The saying 'your reputation precedes you'', applies here.<br />\n<br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTkkiMqVaI/AAAAAAAAByQ/UZj0gQrz8BM/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTkkiMqVaI/AAAAAAAAByQ/UZj0gQrz8BM/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Personal branding can single an individual out as a rock star in his field.</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTkp3wu6TI/AAAAAAAAByU/M_3E1I4mbEM/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTkp3wu6TI/AAAAAAAAByU/M_3E1I4mbEM/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Personal branding is easier than company branding. Your image and mystique is already created - you just have to market it.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">How do you market yourself? You must be THE expert in your field. There must be differentiation\u2014what makes you different?</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTlIwRu4OI/AAAAAAAAByo/fxlFqbEiKBo/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTlIwRu4OI/AAAAAAAAByo/fxlFqbEiKBo/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Your personal brand too travels far and wide, and its reach is almost limitless. Like soliton waves they travel outwards, you don't know how far they will go.&nbsp;</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">A brand is image or a perception. Personal branding is as valuable as corporate branding</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">A brand for a company is like a reputation for a person. A brand is driven by a personal connection and emotion.</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTk4xQ2puI/AAAAAAAAByg/HZ65u5Z72T8/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTk4xQ2puI/AAAAAAAAByg/HZ65u5Z72T8/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Harley Davidson bikers are enthusiastic advocates of their brands because of the high level of involvement they have with them and the high level of satisfaction that this brands delivers. Emotion is one of the most potent weapons for a brand. People yearn for emotion in a increasingly sanitized and faceless world.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Brands create a feeling of fraternity in many ways. Consumers like to me part of a special club . Consumers feel good just about meeting other consumers of the same brand as in the case of a Harley Davidson bike. It is about appeasing their emotional needs. Brand loyalty is indeed the ultimate goal of marketing.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">If Coke is valued at 75 billion, it is NOT the cost of the inventory after depreciation. It is the cost of the brand. It signifies its potential in future profit raking.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Employees are willing to work for a strong brand at less salary . Good brands benefit with a stable work force and hence provide stability to company performance and better share prices.</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTlYwiiuqI/AAAAAAAAByw/A-eLqj2NAvE/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTlYwiiuqI/AAAAAAAAByw/A-eLqj2NAvE/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Mindless marketing like BUY ONE AND TWO FREE can destroy a brand\u2014 Brand equity is the goose that lays golden eggs, therefore don\u2019t go for short term single minded not too bright short term gains and erode the brand equity forever.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">A product\u2019s superiority is in itself no longer sufficient to guarantee its success.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Hence branding is used to fool your gut feeling, by clever advertisements and shrewd marketing experts.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">SOME ADVISE--</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Do not let everyone know everything about you. Cultivate a mystique. If you stand still and stagnate , it is your fault.&nbsp;</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTlPkInX-I/AAAAAAAABys/-EIJy_19E0I/s1600/images+%25289%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTlPkInX-I/AAAAAAAABys/-EIJy_19E0I/s1600/images+%25289%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Leaders never shout--they give orders with firmness and decision. Don\u2019t sweat the small stuff.</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTkym87jRI/AAAAAAAAByc/fh10P37_tEI/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTkym87jRI/AAAAAAAAByc/fh10P37_tEI/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Be your own man without being overly concerned about the reactions of others. Success that cost you your dignity is not an achievement\u2014but a profound personal failure.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Your outward appearance does affect your image.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Protect your personal brand, nobody else will do it for you. When your image improves , your performance improves.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">It takes 30 years to build a rock solid personal brand -- and just takes less than 5 seconds to bring it down like a house of cards. Your knowledge has to be improved, challenged and increased constantly or it vanishes. Avoid leaving things to lady luck.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">In the twilight of your life when all is said and done the quality of your life boils down to the quality of your contribution to others.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Remember, deep down in the heart people appreciate discipline and strength. Keep your gunpowder dry , \u2014 maintain readiness.&nbsp;Romance the stress.</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTk-XTIeHI/AAAAAAAAByk/H6PodMeJ21Y/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTk-XTIeHI/AAAAAAAAByk/H6PodMeJ21Y/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Do things that others do not expect\u2014 that others are not familiar with. Dream big\u2014 but you must be realistic.</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">Make a difference in your field, be world class -- nay-- make a dent in the universe. leave behind a legacy that the storm of time cannot erode.</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTktsief6I/AAAAAAAAByY/w6esAPzKI_A/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQTktsief6I/AAAAAAAAByY/w6esAPzKI_A/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><i><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 18px;\"><b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">When you do the common things in life in an uncommon way, you will command the attention of the world. - George Washington Carver.</span></b></span></i></div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\"><br />\n</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</div><div style=\"margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">..</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "17", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/656070076093330683/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "4628627544419817631", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-12-12T12:02:00+05:30", "updated": "2018-08-01T01:59:09+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTMzMDY4OTQ5NDI4Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/12/deepwell-pumps-on-chemical-tankers-capt.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4628627544419817631", "title": "DEEPWELL PUMPS ON CHEMICAL TANKERS--   CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<br />\n<h1>\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: small;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;FRAMO PUMP AND PUMPING OPERATIONS<o:p></o:p></span></b></h1>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQRsJ6Rl14I/AAAAAAAABwI/Ojx4Nlaz6CI/s1600/P4040081.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQRsJ6Rl14I/AAAAAAAABwI/Ojx4Nlaz6CI/s640/P4040081.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Deepwell pumps have done away with the suction pipeline where 90% of pumping problems lie.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It has almost eliminated cavitation for free flowing liquids. Fluids are broadly classified as Newtonian and non Newtonian depending on their obedience to the laws of classical mechanics. Newtonian fluid/ rate of flow is proportional to the force applied.. <span style=\"color: black;\">Some will not flow till the force exerted is greater than the yield point.</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQSvgOJXQFI/AAAAAAAAByE/_XZUCUyARe8/s1600/013.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQSvgOJXQFI/AAAAAAAAByE/_XZUCUyARe8/s1600/013.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Deepwell pumps on our chemical tankers are mainly Norwegian Framo and Japanese Deepwell types on a few . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">JD ( lets call Japanese deepwell pumps <b>JD</b> \u2014for convenience ) pumps have huge disadvantages over Framo pumps .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">1) The JD SS impeller is locked by a SS washer and nut which can work loose. In Framo a nylon bolt and washer ( disposable ) is used which provides&nbsp; better friction coefficient.&nbsp; A loose impeller can cause explosion.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">2) The JD cargo seal is mechanical while for Framo it is a double lip seal teflon ring. Mechanical seal cannot run dry as it will over heat and get damaged. This overheat is not conducive to safety .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">3) JD pumps do not have a jockey pump which in a Framo system runs round the clock 365 days a year to prevent cargo <i>ingress into <u>hydraulic</u></i> system. Here the cofferdam is pressurised by air/ nitrogen from a fixed pipeline connection to prevent cargo ingress into cofferdam. This serves to cool the mechanical seal too.&nbsp; While on a Framo air blow to purge the cofferdam is from an air&nbsp; flexible. Fixed air connections can cause high density free flowing cargoes like Sulphuric acid to <i>ingress the</i> <u>compressed air lines</u>. Jockey pump provides continious air venting, filtration of hyd oil and prevents moisture ingress. If the JD system does not have a feed/ jockey pump, it is important to purge air from the highest point--- it could be on top of the crane.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">4) Framo uses rotating impeller as a non return valve while stripping stack, while on Japanese models there could be a non return flap just on top of the impeller which is a huge disadvantage when you want to clear the suction pit off sediments by blowing air or steam.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">5) In JD the hydraulic inlet valve is opened only when the cargo tank pump is run. On Framo the ball valve for high pressure inlet is closed only while servicing the pump.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">6) Latest Framo pumps have stripping cones to feed impeller which reduced the rob to less than a litre. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Here we shall talk about a typical Framo system which is fitted on majority of EMS ships :--- <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remember a cargo pump with a blocked cofferdam must never be used. Cofferdam separates the hydraulic system fom the cargo system. The cargo seals consists of upper single cofferdam lipseal and lower double cargo lip seal mounted on ceramic sleeve. Both must be changed together as per Framo recommendation. The wear rings need not be changed unless there is a significant reduction in pump capacity or sweeping party gets affected by cargo spray. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">For 2 power packs you will have&nbsp; have to start the second generator.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Main hyd system pressure must be 15 bars above the highest consumer.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The number of pumps you can use at full speed is governed by the hyd oil consumption of each as per list posted in CCR.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove air from hyd system always at the highest point.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Power pack has vent interlock. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Always start the Framo pump with the dischg valve shut. When starting dischg open the cargo dischg valve only when the dischg pressure is above manifold&nbsp; common pressure ot you will have a backflow.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When there is high back pressure it is better to do internal stripping. If there is no possibility to do this ensure that the dischg from tank is going ashore and not to another tank. For this both the tanks dischg pressure must be higher than the manifold pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is better to run as many pumps in parallel as practicable at a reduced hyd pressure than just a few pumps at max hyd pressure. 2 pumps at 100 % capacity is same as 4 pumps at 50 % capacity. The advantage is reduced hyd system pressure on old ships where the hyd lines are corroded.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When starting screw booster pump ( molasses/ clay slurry ) without bypass ensure that the delivery side valves incl shore tank is open , or you will spring a leak.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Empty tank at reduced pressure. If required throttle delivery valve on deck. This is not reqd if you have a suction well.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When you have suction well and less back pressure like when stripping salt water , as soon as the tank&nbsp; is empty close cargo valve fast and stop pump.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pump speed depends upon backpressure, viscosity and density of cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When using the CCR joystick to discharge make sure the local control STC is fully open ( fully clockwise )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Stripping cannot be done from CCR especially if there is no suction well.-- as it is important to hear the booming sound when the tank gets empty. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Stripping procedure:--<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Keep some body in CCR. Reduce pump hyd pressure to 100 bars when pump loses suction as indicated by pressure fluctuation.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Go on deck and shut STC / FCV&nbsp; ( turn anticlockwise to shut) till hyd pressure drop by 10 bars. You must see the movement of needle. The idea is to avoid surge while transfer of control.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Now the control is on deck.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Tell CCR to fully open the&nbsp; remote flow control joystick lever by pushing it max upward.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Shut cargo delivery valve&nbsp; once you hear the air rushing inside stack.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyText2\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Connect compressed air to stack and strip stack.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyText2\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">( At 7 kg pressure. There is no need to open and shut air as the liquid always remains at bottom and air on top in stack as per the laws of Physics . Ensure air is opened slowly to avoid liquid hammer especially with dense liquids like Sulphuric acid. This can cause the ptfe gasket to creep and spray acid on the stripper. At time of stripping stack 50 bars hyd pressure is enough. Never run Framo pump less than 50 bars. It is not possible on the later models.)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyText2\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Once stack is empty you can hear the pump racing. Shut the STC/ FCV ( turn anticlockwise ) to reduce pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Close cargo dischg valve first.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Then put off pump from CCR by pulling down the&nbsp; remote flow control&nbsp; lever fully.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If the tank is aft of manifold and there is good stern trim then super strip the topline. You must have have Polypropelene super strip hoses. Basically you are transferring liquid from inboard end of shut manifold valve to outboard end.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Purge the cofferdam. Neglecting purging with high mp heated cargoes will result in a blocked cofferdam. Before purging cofferdam check that the relief valve ( lifts at 3 bars ).&nbsp; First drain the compressed air line from the lowest point.&nbsp; Or you get wrong measurement in container. Purge several times , not once. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><b>Purging the cofferdam</b> must be done as a ritual\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">1) Immediately after loading<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">2) 12 hrs after loading<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">3) If leaking purge every day, other wise every 7 days<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">4) If doing recirc like clay , then before after start/ stop.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">5) Before / after dischg.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Fill up the Framo purging log , chief officer must ensure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">No air coming out means a blocked cofferdam. Use steam/ solvent to clear the block. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">To fill up cofferdam with water ( while dischg Molasses etc ) use the same system of purging cofferdam in reverse.&nbsp; This means that the air purging connection must be opened out to vent air out which is displaced by water. For cargoes like clay slurry the water must be recirculated or the cargo seals will get damaged.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><b>Filling up cofferdam</b> with ( to avoid cargo ingress and improve seal life , always ensure hyd return pressure converted to head is higher)---<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Phenol </i>/ caustic recirc hot water. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>TDI/ MDI</i> and polymerising cargo fill up with DOP (VD is 13.5)<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Crystallising cargo</i> like Molasses fill up with FW<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Phosphoric acid</i>/ recirc with FW to remove residue<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Clay slurry/ Kaolin</i> flush cofferdam 3 times daily . Don\u2019t use deepwell pump to strip tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Flushing of cofferdam during dischg of viscous cargoes has cooling effect on friction heat between cargo sleeve and ceramic sleeve.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hyd oil leakage into cofferdam upto 200 ml a day is nothing to worry about.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">For this you have to stand the sample for oil to separate out from mixture.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">For Hyd oil in cofferdam, pressurise the hyd return side. Change mech oil seal or shaft seal. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If cargo leaks into the cofferdam don\u2019t just change the seal. First find out where the leak is from. To pressure test cofferdam blank by rubber gasket the relief valve and test for pressure drop at 3 kg and soap water. 400ml of cargo in cofferdam when pump is running the full day is ok.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is better to superstrip the topline before stripping the pumpstack when you are dealing with viscous Luboils, Molasses etc. This way you are able to strip against the lowest backpressure. For your info Molasses is NEVER loaded through framo pump if there is no filter at ships manifold\u2014there might be the odd old shoe or cane piece coming along. High brix Molasses ( Columbian is 93 ) is usually pumped out by Framo portable screw pump MP125, of head 100 m. The pump can be reversed to dispose off fibres of Molasses in the screws.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">During tankwash ensure the bottom is always dry. Water in must be equal to water out. In the end allow 10 cm of wash water build up by stopping the pump. Then run pump full speed for 3 minutes to flush internal parts. At this time open and shut stripping valve to flush the stripping line.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyText\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Never allow saltwater to remain in pump stack. Always flush with FW.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Every 6 months Framo pump wear test should be carried out. This can be done by running Framo with dischg valve shut as good speed and FW as medium. Wear rings get worn out by running a pump dry. Dry running happens during stripping and tankcleaning. The Framo pumps can be run against a closed cargo valve without an risk of eventual overheating as the wear ring loss comes back into the tank. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The bearings in the Framo cargo pump is lubricated and cooled by hyd return oil and so the pump can run dry without any damage.&nbsp; This means that the hyd return oil temperature is also a bearing monitoring system. An alarm will be activated if the temp is greater than 60 deg C. If temp exceeds 65 deg C all powerpacks are automatically unloaded except one. When temp drops &lt;60 deg C they will be automatically reloaded. System reset button must be activated before any pump can be restarted. The temp is automatically maintained between 30 and 50 deg C by cooling water.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When picking up anchor and for stations keep system pressure sufficiently high.&nbsp; Max main Hyd pressure allowed is around 240 bars. The return to tank is 4 kg.&nbsp; Joint leaks on old ships always happen while starting, due to air bubbles smashing in pressure line, and expansion in return line.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cargo in cofferdam means\u2014cargo seal, ceramic sleeve, pumphead seal leaks.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Ceramic sleeves can be polished. Worn seals can be reconditioned by Framo shore service.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Oil in cofferdam means---mech or lip shaft seal, pumphead seals leaks.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If hyd oil /cargo leakage is too much close hyd valves and use portable Framo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cofferdam seperates cargo section from hyd section.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cargo seal is exposed only to static head from cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Avoid dry running of Framo pumps or steaming stack for more than 10 min.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">To replace a worn shaft bearing the complete pump needs to be withdawn by the shore crane. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><u>The following passage is for better technical understanding</u> of swivel angle/ swash plate and is available in the technical manuals\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Framo power pack load sharing is by ammeter or swash plate angle.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">FCV has been replaced by STC on new Framo systems. STC or speed torque control valve prevent overspeed of pumps. STC regulated hyd pressure and limits the flow of hyd oil to pump motors . The max outflow is adjusted by Framo manufacturer and the adj screw is sealed. If the seal is broken the warrantly claims will not be honoured. The construction of a hyd motor is exactly the same as the hyd pump. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pilot pressure controller:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">To keep a balance between oil delivery and consumption a PCV is needed. This valve is a stepless remote control from CCR. When system pressure reached the set value of the PCV , the valve will open for oil to the pump angle control cylinder. The swivel angle will now balance out. If the oil consumption from the cargo pump is increased, system pressure will drop slightly and oil flow through the PCV will drop. The swivel angle will now increase until a new balance is achieved between oil delivery and consumption. By means of this system , oil delivery will always remain same as oil consumption. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The coarse filter on the suction side of the powerpack pump is 100 microns while the fine filter on the delivery side of pump is 10 microns. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The flow into the cargo pump hydraulic motor is regulated by FCV. The control signal into this valve can be adjusted locally ( deck ) or remotely ( CCR ) with the motor rpm depending upon hyd delivery pressure. Varying hyd pressure varies motor rpm. In closed system the level of hyd pressure is fed back to the control side of pump. This signal adjusts the swash plate of the pump adjusting the delivered hyd oil quantity. The pilot pump supplies the desired hyd pressure signal to the swash plate control and thus signal is adjustable. The feed pump maintains a slight positive pressure on the suction side of the pump and should only deliver fluid when the main system has some leakage or the hyd oil contracts due to lowering temp. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Keep the special Framo tools like\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Antirotating tool for impeller hub<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Extractors for impeller/ hub/ sleeve / hyd motor<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Assembling cylinder<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Mech seal assembler<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Drain tool<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Drain pump<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Jack <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Lifting bolts<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Mirror<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Plastic strips<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Etc in a safe place and not mixed up with other tools<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent3\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When loading through the Framo pump must the manufacturers rates be NEVER be exceeded. When planning the loading rate the density of the cargo must be considered to avoid possible irreparable damage to the submerged pump. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent3\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In case a cofferdam is blocked\u2014no air returned while purging\u2014inform the chemical operator.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent3\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">NEVER use abrupt and sudden movements of the Framo joystick in the CCR. When starting discharge, keep pump at slow speed until all checks have been completed, before increasing pump speed. When discharging against high back pressure\u2014do internal stripping.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyTextIndent3\" style=\"margin-left: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When tankcleaning , the cargo pump stripping capacity should be balanced against the volume of washing water being introduced to the tank. <b><i><u>NEVER OPERATE THE CARGO PUMP DRY</u></i></b><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><b>Simple rules for the correct operation of the Framo Pumps</b><b><i><o:p></o:p></i></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">1 Purge cofferdam, before during and after use.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">2 Check back pressure in return filters and in oil cooler.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">3 Refill the oil tank through the filter box.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">4 Drain off any water or sediment in the oil tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">5 Slow down pump when tank cleaning.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<h1 style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: small;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: large;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;PORTABLE FRAMO PUMP</span></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></h1>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
