text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQRsOo-zmAI/AAAAAAAABwM/eLJMyXMxfME/s1600/clockwise+shut+portable+framo+.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"478\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQRsOo-zmAI/AAAAAAAABwM/eLJMyXMxfME/s640/clockwise+shut+portable+framo+.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQSw1rJTCCI/AAAAAAAAByI/im1UIyQ2GGI/s1600/P8200009.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"478\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQSw1rJTCCI/AAAAAAAAByI/im1UIyQ2GGI/s640/P8200009.JPG\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If a vessel is fitted with individual deepwell pumps, then she will also be required to carry at least one portable pump.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The pumps should be tested at least 4 times a year and hydraulic couplings on deck should be identified, kept operational and covered with denso-tape.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The use of the portable pump occurs when a main tank pump fails and the tank can only be discharged using the emergency procedures.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The use of the portable pump is a labour intensive and high risk operation, which can be further compounded by the nature of the chemical to be discharged.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If the emergency pump is to be used, then the terminal and owners should be advised.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The terminal should also be aware of any problems anticipated and co-operation and communication is vital for the safe and efficient discharge of the cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The pump described below is a FRAMO TK4. If another type of pump is on board, then the particular operation of that pump is to be used.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">There are basically three main components which make up the portable pump.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">1 The pump unit.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">2 The starter head with hoses between pump and head.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">3 Pressure and return hoses between the starter head and the snap on coupling stations on deck.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Flexible hoses of sufficient length are coupled to the pump to effect the discharge. The length of flexible hose should be kept to the minimum to reach the installed pipework.<b><o:p></o:p></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: -1.0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.5in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; The portable pump is lowered into the cargo tank by a sling and not by the hydraulic hoses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: -1.0in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -.5in;\">\n<br /></div>\n<h1 style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: small;\">PORTABLE FRAMO TRY OUT<o:p></o:p></span></b></h1>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQRsSqMLKwI/AAAAAAAABwQ/twjdQO93B9E/s1600/portable+framo.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQRsSqMLKwI/AAAAAAAABwQ/twjdQO93B9E/s640/portable+framo.jpg\" width=\"478\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">As soon as a new Chief officer/ Pumpman joins he should at the earliest rig up the portable Framo pump and try it out. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Never hook up without a flow control valve for speed control and stop/ start.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A) Fill up a empty 200 litre drum with SW and keep a couple of fire hoses standby to fill it up.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">B) Use tripod the same way you will use in a tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">C) Before connecting hyd hoses close flow control valve. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">D) Check for cleanliness on snap on couplings.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">E) Always connect return hyd hose first--- \u2018and open valve\u2019.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">F) Connect pressure hyd hose and open valve.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">G) Open flow control valve till the required rpm is reached, don\u2019t let the drum go dry. If so then put dischg back into the drum.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">H) Probable&nbsp; specs of a portable framo will be 180 bars/ 70 cum&nbsp; per hour/ 140 ltrs hyd oil per min<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I) After you are satisfied , rinse with FW.&nbsp; Then&nbsp; first shut flow control valve.&nbsp; Make system pressure zero.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">J) Close pressure line valve first and then return.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">K) Always disconnect pressure hyd hose first and then return.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">L) Before keeping back in store release the oil pressure inside hyd hoses by removing about 20 CC of oil, by pushing with fingers.&nbsp; Otherwise in an actual emergency you will have difficulty in connecting the snap on couplings.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">M) Don\u2019t kink the hoses in the store.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Portable Framo pump is not used to pump ashore. Rather it is used to pump from one tank whose pump does not work to another tank of the same grade or empty tank whose pump works.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If the emergency pump is to be used, then the terminal and chemical operator should be advised. The terminal should also be aware of any problems anticipated and mutual co-operation is vital for the safe and efficient discharge of the cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Ensure that only the lower half of the pump is submerged and is lowered as the cargo level falls .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-size: large;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<b>FRAMO DEEPWELL PUMP OVERHAULING<o:p></o:p></b></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">MODELS: SD125&nbsp; AND SD150 ( design number 5 )<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Shut inlet valve of main hydraulic inlet pressure line.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Purge the cofferdam.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"border-bottom: double windowtext 6.75pt; border: none; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; mso-border-bottom-alt: thin-thick-thin-medium-gap windowtext 6.75pt; mso-element: para-border-div; padding: 0in 0in 0in 0in;\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"border: none; mso-border-bottom-alt: thin-thick-thin-medium-gap windowtext 6.75pt; mso-padding-alt: 0in 0in 0in 0in; padding: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Take the Framo tool box down.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"border: none; mso-border-bottom-alt: thin-thick-thin-medium-gap windowtext 6.75pt; mso-padding-alt: 0in 0in 0in 0in; padding: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">To dismantle impeller and wear rings:<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove 8 nos bolts to dismantle pump support ring.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Lift up the support ring and tie it up with a rope about one metre high.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Loosen 8 nos bolts of upper wear ring support.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Then loosen 2 turns only 6 nos allen bolts for impeller hub (inner ).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Turn impeller clockwise for easy access.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Press down the bolts and impeller.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When impeller is loose remove the bolts.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove 4 nos bolts between volute casing and cargo leg.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Replace 2 of the bolts with long lifting bolts---one bolt on each leg.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove remaining bolts between volute casing and bearing housing of cargo flange.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Now all volute casing , impeller and suction cover is hanging on lifting bolts diagonally positioned on each cargo leg.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Lower unit on plastic strips.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Slide the unit out of the well.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove upper wear ring and inspect it ( white large ring ).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove black o ring and small white seal element between impeller and impeller hub.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Put unit upside down<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove nuts between suction cover and impeller.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Inspect white wear ring. Normal radial clearance is 0.2 mm. if clearance becomes greater than 1mm renew.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Loosen locking bracket and remove locking ring.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Fit back the suction bellmouth to lift up the suction cone<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Finally lift up the impeller. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Note; wear rings usually last 10 years for clean oils. For sediment cargoes like clay slurry you will have to renew often.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">To dismantle double cargo lip seal and cofferdam seal:<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">First dismantle 4 bolts on the lower part of thin cofferdam check pipe.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Put a mirror.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Dismantle impeller hub from the pump shaft.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Loosen lock washer.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove bolt and pull out impeller hub.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Use extractor to remove impeller hub.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Don\u2019t damage or ring and ceramic sleeve.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Put on the assembling cylinder to keep the ceramic sleeve in place and protect seal lips.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pull down seal ring housing with cargos seal.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove the thin white Teflon seal ring.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove (thick small with spring) double cargo lip seal.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove single lip cargo seal.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Note : always change single and double cargo lip seal together as they come as one spare part.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove ceramic sleeve after removing the assembling cylinder.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">To dismantle Mech oil seal :<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Mech seal can be dismantled without draining oil from the hyd pump stack.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remove bearing housing from pump casing.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Put upside down and remove upper seal ring housing.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Use 2 lifting bolts and remove mech seal stationary part ( black ) and Teflon seal element.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Use special tool for rotating part of mech sealnever use grease on oring of stationary seal---use soap water.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Dismantle pumpshaft, ball bearing and back stop unit ( after reading the manual ).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">For hyd motor you must drain out hyd oil from pump stack.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Use air driven drain pump given by Framo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Lower hyd motor by using Framo jack.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Assembling<br />\n<br />\n<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Assembling is done the reverse way the things came off.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">However turn ceramic sleeve by 180 degrees.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Groove from double lip cargo seal must be facing towards the impeller.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Fit retainer ring on geared shaft correctly at end of ceramic sleeve.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Running test:<o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pressure test cofferdam at 3 bars pressure. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Blank cofferdam vent pipe.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Unscrew the complete air relief valve and connect pressure guage.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Check for pressure drop . Pressure must be stable for 30 minutes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\">FRAMO HARDWARE <o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQRsXXXyivI/AAAAAAAABwU/RQeuV8TVa8Y/s1600/DSC07863.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQRsXXXyivI/AAAAAAAABwU/RQeuV8TVa8Y/s640/DSC07863.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When a new delivery Master or Chief Engineer goes to the yard to take over a ship , they must know the following minimum essentials.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">They must know which hardware is yard supply and what is Framo supply. The Framo supply is usually perfect, the yard supply and the interfacing needs to be checked in great detail\u2014this is why they are sent by company to the yard well in advance. The new building superintendent is of course there much before, and he need to read this chapter too. &nbsp;Sometimes for yard\u2019s convenience they do not fit Framo supply hardware, and this must be rectified.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">For example, recently when one of our Masters pointed out to the yard, that the Framo air purge couplings for stripping the stack do not have non return ball valves ( but wrongly fitted with yard supply shut off cocks ) as is usual for Framo fitted ships as a Framo supply&nbsp; , the yard initially stonewalled\u2014but since this was done in writing with copy to Framo and company, the yard was forced to recify it free of cost before delivery. Imagine Sulphuric acid spraying on the Pumpmans face, after he finished stripping the stack!!.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Look for alien voltage from interfaced equipment prior to working. There must be sufficient service space and lifting hook pad eyes. Hydraulic oil used must be mineral based and must have FP between 180 and 230 C.&nbsp; This was another mistake recently noticed---the yard had to drain out the cheap quality yard supply hydraulic oil , flush the system and then fill up again with the correct viscocity/ FP hydraulic oil ,as specified by Framo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Any hyd leak spray must not come in contact with heated surfaces. Check hyd oil connections, valves and flanges\u2014if necessary put splash tapes on flanges. If the power pack is in the ER\u2014an oil mist detector is desirable. This is bound to be a regulation very soon.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Welding on framo equipment in not to be done without permission.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">There must be no paint on flexible hoses and rubber dampers\u2014as it will crack very soon.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is important to know the hyd oil conspumption of all cargo pumps\u2014big and small , ballast pumps, &nbsp;portable pump, &nbsp;tankcleaning pump etc in litres/ minute. &nbsp;This must be posted at the remore panel in the CCR.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Any consumer hooked on to the central hydraulic ring , main system can be run ( like crane ) as long as the oil delivery is sufficient. To control the speed of the hyd motor a FCV ( old ships ) / STC ( all&nbsp; new ships ) &nbsp;is fitted. Framo does not make FCV any more\u2014they make it only for the portable pumps.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Check the hydraulic oil storage tank and clean oil drain tank. Both must have sloping bottoms away from the suction and towards the bottom drain for efficient water draining. These tanks are usually yard supply\u2014the rest are Framo supply.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In case the power pack is situated outside the ER, the ventilation must be sufficient\u2014without ingress of salt spray. The advantage of having the power pack in the higher level FP store is the natural head of hydraulic oil afforded , to the mechanical hydraulic oil seal at cofferdam of submerged cargo pump,&nbsp; in case the Jockey pump fails.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">There must be an obstruction free arrangement in case the whole pipe stack and pump head has to be removed from the tank with a tall crane.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The pipestack must be parallel to the bulkhead, where the bracket for the intermediate support is welded.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">From Framo CCR control\u2014you should be able to see manifold\u2014the console is made by yard.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Look for dents on framo pump risers \u2013due to incorrect handling by slings or forklift marks under power pack units ( they must be lifted by 4 hooks ). The risers have concentric pipes inside inlet/ return/ cofferdam.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Framo pumps must be installed only after the welding causing spatter, grinding, pickling in the tanks are over in SS tanks -- or for the matter ,painting in coated tanks.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Note\u2014Framo recommends hyd drums to be stored horizontally when it is kept out door\u2014so that the bungs are covered by oil\u2014oil can leak out\u2014but water cannot come in.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Water has a negative effect on hyd oil additives , which have been primarily put to improve oil quality.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Framo drops must not lead to pump suction\u2014it must not hit steam coils\u2014must slip underneath and hit the forward bulkhead for tsunami recirculation.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Flexible hoses for stack stripping will have SS snap on couplings, with a NR &nbsp;ball valve at each end. The hose will not be &gt; 2 metres long, will be SS braided, will be heavy duty and hard to bend at 180 deg angles. There will be NO jubilee clips\u2014if you notice Jubilee clips it is a deliberate yard mistake. They have fitted a compressed air outlet valve far away from the pump, and instead of relocating the air valve they did the next best in a clandestine manner\u2014that is, give the ship a longer hose with couplings fixed by jubilee clamps. After stripping the stack there must be no need to shut a cock before disconnecting. Cargo must not ingress the air flexible even if air pressure drops from 7 kg.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Exhaust traps must have 50 cms clearance to keep a collecting bucket . Cofferdam blow is done into a compatible bucket and not into the clear sample glass bottle. There must be different buckets for different grades of cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The intermediate riser supports must no be welded in corners or slope of corrugated solid steel \u2013or on 2 different bulkheads at corners of tank. Framo have certain calculations on which they decide whether to put one or two intermediate riser supports. Be aware in tanks without sloshing considerations and less load density,&nbsp; carriage of free flowing high density cargoes like sulphuric acid of SG-1.85 can cause cracks. Master must prevent ship from rolling excessively and not trust the Framo calculations to deliver his tanks from cracking danger . Framo calculations have not taken into account the ships tanks\u2019 load density\u2014if a heavy cargo of 2.0 SG can be loaded 98% or partially full.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Prior pump installation the deck trunk and brackets for intermediate and bottom support have to be welded into the tank. A good yard will use a Framo provided dummy with laser beam holes to avoid templating misalignment. Good alignment means no cracks. While the Japanese yards are experts in this\u2014newly mushroomed yards who have jumped into the fray with the chemical Type 2 tanker veg oil shipping boom ( after 1.1.2007 ) may not be so. In such yards the Owners yard new building superintendent must carry his own laser pencil beam\u2014available in the market.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Welding seams of deck trunks must not be facing the ship side where they can get pounded by a incompressible green water wave.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Ammeters must be be provided for motors &gt; 7.5 KW. A good chief engineer who knows about swash plate angles of variable displacement Framo power pack pumps will hardly need this Ammeter.&nbsp; The ratio of current transformer must be told to Framo by yard if an ampere meter is required on the hydraulic system control panel.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cables for motor heating elements and thermistors must not be interchanged as voltage &gt;2.5V will damage the thermistors. &nbsp;Motor heating elements must be powered up immediately after installation.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hydraulic oil tanks must be vented indoors repeat indoors -and that too with an air filter, not to outer decks. The storage volume must be min 50% of the total oil volume in the hydraulic system\u2014the recommended is 70%.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The storage and clean oil drain tank must be SS to prevent coating\u2014if not grit blast to SA2.5 and give two coats of hyd oil resistant epoxy 100 microns each. Only SS pipes are used, copper or galvanized pipes must never be used.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Manometer test connections must be provided by the yard at both supply and return lines, to do trouble shooting and to test for pressure peaks.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Venting plugs must be at the highest point\u2014at both pressure and return pipes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Framo does not accept hydraulic&nbsp; cylinders connected to the system. If &nbsp;a crane has to be used they recommend a separate hyd system with hyd motor driven from Framo system. But as long as the CCR OOW is aware that a crane is being operated , he can be vigilant.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pipelines must not have too much of pressure drop ( smooth internal surface ) or air pockets. Framo pressure drop calculations are based on minimum ID .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Unnecessary flanges must be avoided by yard. All pipeline spool welds must be possible to be inspected from a flange\u2014say using a video scope, at the yard.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The resilient pipeline clamps must have 4 rubber pads at all 4 quadrants\u2014equally compressed to absorb vibrations and prevent transmission to deck structures. These clamps must be welded to rigid structure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pipeline bulkhead penetrations must be resilient Framo supply. The inner bulkhead must have a protection cup,, lined with glass wool.\u2014both yard supply.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Expansion loops on hyd pipelines must be always horizontal\u2014never vertical. &nbsp;These are for thermal expansion and axial forces/ deflection of ship\u2019s structure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Water ballast pumps must be connected to different RCV blocks\u2014to ensure operation of ballast system if one valve block is out of service.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pilot pipes on open decks must be made of SS.&nbsp; Pilot pipes min distance between expansion loops is 25 metres. If attached to the catwalk\u2014expansion loop must correspond with the expansion joint. If there are 2 tiers there must be no contact between any pipe and adjacent flange\u2014flanges can be turned to avoid contact. Only cold bending is permitted.\u2014free of wrinkles on inner side and 7%&nbsp; ovalty. Pipes must be degreased before bending and pickled after bending. Low pressure pipes have Teflon mandril inside the pipes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">TIG welding with Argon gas is recommended for SS. Carbon steel pipes must be coated with zinc rich epoxy. Neutralization of carbon steel pipes after pickling\u20142% phosphoric acid at 85 deg C for 5 min, the Framo way is wrong\u2014Nitric acid would have been the best.&nbsp; Neutralization of SS ( passivation ) 14% Nitric acid at ambient temp for 45 min.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pipe clamps must be welded only AFTER alignment and assembly of pipes. Adjusting spools are min 2 to 3 metres long\u2014the pipes must be pulled apart before inserting to prevent damage to spool O ring. Use Molebnenum Sulphide grease on screw connections.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">As soon as you join the ship \u2013check the manifold\u2014if the manifold athwartship pipes are &nbsp;above the fore and aft cargo deck lines it simplifies the loading. If it is below\u2014it simplifies the stripping. This&nbsp; knowledge is vital with high MP cargoes loaded from barges in freezing weather\u2014like Phenol loading / dischg in winter. If pipelines get frozen with toxic cargo and you have to put you crew in danger to unfreeze the lines\u2014it is a disgrace.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If the manifolds are above deck lines\u2014then separate drain lines have to be installed for all deck pipelines.&nbsp; If the manifold common collector is above the manifold pipelines\u2014then 2 drain tanks at the manifold.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Hyd oil pour point should be around -26 deg C, with viscosity ISO VG46\u2014the trade name whether it is TELLUS--Shell/ RANDO--Texaco or BARTRAN\u2014BP&nbsp; will have the number 46. The hyd oil must always be filtered by using the Framo hyd oil transfer unit when the oil is filled into the system from the storage tank. Water content must be below 300 ppm or 0.03%<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Air in the system is indicated by \u2013<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Back flow into the system when at standstill<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Great difference in tank level at low and high system pressure<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Foaming<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Discoloured oil<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cooling water pipelines are fitted with flexible bellows to prevent vibrations. Piping at the outlet side must be routed above the oil cooler and a vacuum breaker must be installed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The tank risers have concentric hyd pipes for max safety. Framo cofferdam is at atmospheric pressure, unlike the Japanese deepwell pumps who use air pressurized cofferdams to make up for the lack of Jockey pump\u2014and that too with a fixed air connection!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Remember Framo cargo double lip seal faces only static pressure. Framo pump design permits dry running during stripping and tankcleaning. It facilitates in tank replacement of wear and tear parts without interfering with hydraulic section.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">By purging only the condition of the double seal cargo seal is known, hence replace both single lip and double lip cargo seals together always.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">After fixing the snap on&nbsp; hydraulic couplings of portable framo, secure it with locking ring\u2014only then the arrangement is safe.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Portable Framo TK80 usually provided on board EMS ships have a capacity of 90 cum/ hr. Portable &nbsp;Framo inlet pressure is usually 180 bars and the &nbsp;return line pressure 16 bars. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Before purging cofferdam drain the compressed air supply line off water. When purging cofferdam the cofferdam relief valve operates at 3.5 bars. If not, then you get air into the hydraulic system with once the air pressure is greater than the jockey pump pressure, due to a blocked cofferdam. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Light cargoes like Methanol/ Naphtha bypass cargo seals and penetrate cofferdams more easily than viscous ones like Lub oils/ Veg oils. &nbsp;Cofferdam ingress of cargo volume means nothing, if the type of cargo purged is not mentioned.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Non viscous cargo leakage 0.5 litres/ day is normal. Oil leakage 0.25 litres / day is normal.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cargo leakage in cofferdam can be\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Wear on ceramic sleeve<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Leaking pump stack/ pumphead seals<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">To fill up a cofferdam prior dischg, for cargoes like Caustic soda\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Disconnect exhaust trap piping from pump top plate\u2014use a suitable adaptor and fill up.\u2014allow air to escape from snap on air coupling \u2013in other words this is reverse of purging<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">For continious circulation of water while discharging ,for cargoes like Clay slurries:--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Same way as you blow the cofferdam. Ensure the hyd return oil pressure is higher than the cofferdam&nbsp; pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If the hyd oil temp is &lt;20C circulate the oil for heating at max 100 bars prior to raising the pressure to 150 bars.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When using deck mounted heaters \u2013make sure the cargo is circulating though the heater before opening steam inlet valve. Never heat without necessary cargo flow through the heater to avoid carbonizing. Shut off heating medium before the pump is stopped. For deck mounted heaters do NOT heat while discharging\u2014or cargo will come back into the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Jockey pump also prevents water entry into hydraulic oil from leaking cooler.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If oil temp is &lt;20C, circulate the oil though the heating/ venting valve \u2013with one power pack running.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Manual override:--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Mode one--1)Sensor on oil tank is indicating shut down level, and it has been determined that level is OK<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">2)A limit switch is indicating closed valve and it has been verified that the valve is fully open.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Mode 2\u2014for PLC failure<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cooling water valven for power pack is automatic , 50C open\u201430C shut<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Framo pumps can be run against a closed cargo valve without any risk of eventual overheating as the wear ring loss is led directly back into the tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">PCV is a proportional valve for precise and fast control of pressure. This valve is primarily used for remote control of pilot pressure to a Framo hyd control valve. PCV is a compact unit with integrated electronics and a pressure transducer for controlling the pressure on port A. when the current to PCV is zero the spool is in spring return position.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When the actual pressure at port A is lower than the set pressure, the spool will more so that port P and port A are connected, while port T ( to tank ) will close. The valve is then in supply mode.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A limitation is built into the electronics so that the PCV will not open unless the command signal exceeds a pressure of 10-12 bars. The valve closes when the command signal gets lower than 10 bars. When using remote control PCV, the local control valve must be set in max position and vice versa. &nbsp;Everybody on the ship must know this\u2014when a tank is being discharged in bulk or at sea , the local control valve STC must be fully open or fully clockwise. The command signal to the valve is usually set by a potentiometer at the control panel.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Emergency over ride\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This procedure must be known to Chief engineer. Read the Framo manual as soon as you join, and familiarize how to do it, where the allen key has to be inserted and how it has to be turned after loosening the check nut.&nbsp;&nbsp; If you do this simple procedure fast, the chief officer need not rig up the labour intensive portable Framo and end up with ROB and a mandatory and costly pre-wash. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">If the valve has an electrical fault you can mechanically connect port P to port A, and run the cargo pump from local control. Remember to unload local control valve before changing to manual override. Use an allen key\u2014clockwise. After operations connect port A to port T ( tank ) by screwing counter clockwise. Fasten the locknut\u2014don\u2019t use force with allen key.</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 10pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc3zprmmQI/AAAAAAAAB34/qp5PZ969fBw/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc3zprmmQI/AAAAAAAAB34/qp5PZ969fBw/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in; margin-left: 25.0pt; margin-right: 45.45pt; margin-top: 0in; text-align: justify;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 10pt;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: 10pt;\">..</span></div>\n</div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt.
