Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">There are cargoes like Acrylic acid or Propelene Oxide ( violent polymerization ) which may have to be jettisoned for safety of LIFE at sea.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Jettison must be done in concurrence with the Chemical operator , unless an explosion is imminent and time does not permit.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Engine room personnel should be alerted. Consideration should be given to changing over engine room intakes from high to low level and&nbsp; to opposite side of ship.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">All non-essential intakes should be closed.&nbsp;&nbsp; Set up water spray curtains with fire hoses , if relevant.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Not to be done underwater\u2014but discharge from manifold with cargo hose set out as much as possible and as close to water level.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Engine sea suction must be from opposite side.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Make sure wind is from aft and go astern<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">All safety precautions , which involve the presence of flammable/toxic gas in the vicinity of the deck, must be observed. Keep SCBA bottles, EEBD, Oxygen resuscitators in readiness.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">A GMDSS&nbsp; warning should be broadcast.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Crew involved must wear PPE.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Potential sources for ignition must be verified.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Every year one \u201cjettison\u201d emergency drill shall be reported to OOPS as a \u2018QI Notification\u2019, on Chemical tankers.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><u><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">A SAMPLE PROCEDURE:</span></u><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">--<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">ACRYLIC ACID JETTISON PROCEDURE <o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">A:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Should the Cargo Temperature rise to 34C, inform the chemical operator.</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Begin checking the temperature every 30 minutes. Plot on graph paper. Notify Goodwood.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">If adjacent tanks or any tanks in vicinity are being heated stop heating these tanks. If adjacent tanks are empty fill those with ballast if possible, provided sea water temperature is between 18-30C.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Line up for circulation either through existing drop line or rig portable hoses. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 13.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">B.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Should the cargo temperature rise to 41C.</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Begin circulation of the cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Continue temperature monitoring. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">C.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Should the cargo temperature rise to 45C.</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Prepare to pump cargo overboard.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Add cold fresh water to tank as void space permits. Continue circulation. Continue adding fresh water until tank is full, as fresh water supply permits. Closely monitor temperature.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">NOTE: SALT WATER WILL NOT DISSOLVE POLYMER MAKING PUMPING MORE DIFFICULT.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">D.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; Finally at 49C do not wait \u2013 Jettison\u2014</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">&nbsp;<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; color: red;\">DO IT !- &nbsp;IF YOU WIMP OUT, YOU LOSE LIFE YOU WERE ENTRUSTED WITH!!</span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Begin pumping cargo overboard.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">Continue adding fresh water while cargo is being discharged overboard, as FW supply permits.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top: 12.0pt; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-autospace: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt;\">When tank is empty start cleaning with cold water and continue cleaning until tank is clean.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><table border=\"1\" cellpadding=\"0\" cellspacing=\"0\" class=\"MsoNormalTable\" style=\"border-bottom-style: none;
